[2021-12-09 18:41:25] => ::1  => 1  =>  SELECT t.*, bf.branch_name as tbf, bt.branch_name as tbt,g.grade FROM teachers t
      LEFT JOIN branch bf ON bf.branch_id = t.transferred_branch_from
      LEFT JOIN branch bt ON bt.branch_id = t.transferred_branch_to
      LEFT JOIN grade g ON g.grade_id = t.grade_id
